narrative_event = {
	id = wikid.1
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.1
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.1" #Old man and a Map
	picture = GFX_evt_monk_illuminating_book
	
	ai = no
	only_playable = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_ambition = obj_obtain_valyrian_sword
		is_nomadic = no
		OR = {
			is_female = no
			culture_group = hyrkoon_group
			martial = 10
			trait = ambitious	
			trait = proud
			trait = authoritative
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = obj_valyrian_sword } 
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_quest_started } 
			had_character_flag = { flag = wikid_quest_started days = 3650 }
		}
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		NOT = { trait = kingsguard }
		NOT = { trait = nightswatch }	
		in_command = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 180

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			wealth = 250
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			wealth = 500
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			wealth = 1000
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.1" # Let's hear what he has to say.
		trigger = { has_ambition = obj_obtain_valyrian_sword }
		hidden_tooltip = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.2 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.1" # Kick him out of my castle!
		trigger = { has_ambition = obj_obtain_valyrian_sword }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "You are a cheating scumbag."  # Death IRL
		trigger = { NOT = { has_ambition = obj_obtain_valyrian_sword } }
	}
}

	desc = EVTDESCwikid.3 #Old man says go here bring a companion

		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.3" # I am ready and prepared to undertake this 
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.4 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.4 }
		clr_character_flag = wikid_quest_started 
		set_character_flag = wikid_quest_started	
		set_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword
		if = { #recent doom valyria
			limit = { NOT = { year = 7950 } }

		}
	}

			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.4
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.4 #you think and choose
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.4" #The Fellowship of House [ROOT.GetOnlyDynastyName]
	picture = GFX_tutors

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.5 days = 7 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.4" #  Bring me a great warrior		
		capital_scope = {
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { ai = no }
					create_random_soldier = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = NONE
						female = no
						religion = ROOT
						culture = PREV
						name = Fashbinder
						trait = brave
						trait = strong	
						historical = yes
					}
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { ai = yes }
					create_random_soldier = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = NONE
						female = no
						religion = ROOT
						culture = PREV
						trait = brave
						trait = strong	
						historical = yes
					}
				}
				new_character = {
					random_list = {
						10 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
						33 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
						10 = { add_trait = master_warrior }
					}
					random = {
						chance = 25
						add_trait = quick
					}
					set_character_flag = fash_can_be_inbred
					character_event = { id = wikid.499 }
					if = {
						limit = { religion = the_seven }
						knight_character_effect = yes
					}				
				}
			}	
		}		
		set_character_flag = wikid_warrior
	}

character_event = { #give companion random parent to avoid culling
	id = wikid.499

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid.326_new_man } }
			set_character_flag = wikid_companion
		}
		remove_trait = imbecile
		remove_trait = inbred
		remove_trait = slow
		remove_trait = infirm
		remove_trait = incapable
		remove_trait = leper
		remove_trait = possessed
		remove_trait = ill
		remove_trait = pneumonic
		remove_trait = maimed
		remove_trait = crippled
		remove_trait = content
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { age = 20 } }
			create_character = {
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = NONE
				female = no
				age = 36
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			new_character = {
				ROOT = { set_father = PREV }
				death = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				age = 20
				NOT = { age = 35 } 
			}
			create_character = {
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = NONE
				female = no
				age = 51
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			new_character = {
				ROOT = { set_father = PREV }
				death = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { age = 35 }
			create_character = {
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = NONE
				female = no
				age = 66
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			new_character = {
				ROOT = { set_father = PREV }
				death = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = fash_can_be_inbred }
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_trait = inbred }
				99 = { }
			}
			clr_character_flag = fash_can_be_inbred
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.6
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.6 # you leave
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.6" #The Departed
	picture = GFX_evt_trade_post_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.7 days = 30 random = 30 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.6" #  You leave
		add_trait = wikid
		set_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			add_trait = wikid
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
			set_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.51 days = 1000 } }#fail safe
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.8
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.8
	picture = GFX_evt_monk_illuminating_book
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.8" #  HAPPY TIMES
		from = { character_event = { id = wikid.9 days = 2 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = lustful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = hedonist
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { trait = fair }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = chaste
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = celibate
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = 10 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = 40 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = 55 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = wol_seducer_1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.25
				FROM = { has_character_modifier = wol_seducer_2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5.0
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						trait = seducer
						trait = seductress
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.8" #  Pls no
		from = { character_event = { id = wikid.10 days = 2 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
				
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { trait = ugly }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = -10 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = -40 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { personal_opinion = { who = FROM value = -55 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.9
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.9
	picture = GFX_sansa
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.9" #  Yay
		FROM = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like multiplier = 2 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { trait = stressed }
			remove_trait = stressed
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { trait = depressed }
			remove_trait = depressed
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { trait = wounded }
			remove_trait = wounded
		}	
		#remove_trait = maimed ##yeah kinda op but this quest chain uses wound/maim as death chance factors.
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { #pirates
					trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_quest_claim_valyria } }
					narrative_event = { id = wikid.20 days = 50 random = 25 } 
				}
				50 = { #new tangent
					narrative_event = { id = wikid.80 days = 50 random = 25 }
				}
			}	
		}
		set_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_seduce
	}	
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.12
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.12
	picture = GFX_evt_battle
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTZwikid.12" #  WIN CYVASSE evtoptZ
		trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_3 }
		character_event = { id = wikid.16 }
	}

		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.12" #  Attack Dragon with Archer

		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_1 }
			set_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { not = { has_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_1 } }
			set_character_flag = wikid_cyvasse_1
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
				character_event = { id = wikid.11 }
			}	
		}

		}
		if = {

#I have beaten my companion FROMFROM
character_event = {
	id = wikid.181
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.181
	picture = GFX_trial_by_combat
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_from_from = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.181" #  End Quest
		trigger = { FROMFROM = { is_alive = no } }
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.51 days = 30 random = 15 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.51 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.181" #  Practice makes Perfect
		trigger = { FROMFROM = { is_alive = yes } }
		set_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_duel
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { #pirates
					trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_quest_claim_valyria } }
					narrative_event = { id = wikid.20 days = 50 random = 25 } 
				}
				50 = { #new tangent
					narrative_event = { id = wikid.80 days = 50 random = 25 }
				}
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = skilled_warrior }
			random = {
				chance = 10
				hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = skilled_warrior }
				add_trait = master_warrior
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = trained_warrior }
			random = {
				chance = 20
				hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = trained_warrior }
				add_trait = skilled_warrior
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOR = {
					trait = trained_warrior 
					trait = skilled_warrior
					trait = master_warrior
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = poor_warrior }
			add_trait = trained_warrior
		}
	}	
}

			}	
		}

	}

#A fight with the pirates!
character_event = {
	id = wikid.26
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.26
	picture = GFX_knights
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {				
				trait = pirate
				prisoner = no
				war = no
				combat_rating = 2
				age = 16
				NOT = { has_severe_disability_trigger = yes }
				ai = yes
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_pirate1
			save_event_target_as = wikid_pirate1
			break = yes
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {				
				trait = pirate
				prisoner = no
				war = no
				combat_rating = 2
				age = 16
				NOT = { has_severe_disability_trigger = yes }
				is_female = no
				ai = yes
				liege = { ai = yes }
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_pirate1
			save_event_target_as = wikid_pirate1
			break = yes
		}
		e_rebels = { 
			holder_scope = {	
				create_random_soldier = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = NONE
					female = no
					religion = pirate
					culture = lysene
					#name = "Captain Spack Jarrow"
					trait = pirate
				}
				new_character = {
					remove_trait = inbred
					remove_trait = imbecile
					remove_trait = infirm
					remove_trait = incapable
					remove_trait = dwarf
					remove_trait = hunchback
					remove_trait = clubfooted
					remove_trait = weak
					remove_trait = leper
					remove_trait = possessed
					remove_trait = ill
					remove_trait = pneumonic
					remove_trait = maimed
					random_list = {
						30 = { add_trait = poor_warrior }
						30 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
						30 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
						10 = { add_trait = master_warrior }
					}
					add_trait = one_eyed #cool pirates!!
					save_event_target_as = wikid_pirate1
					set_character_flag = wikid_pirate1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.26" # I will fight
		set_character_flag = wikid_player_vs_pirate
		set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
		event_target:wikid_pirate1 = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_suprize_attacked_pirates } 
				}
				add_trait = wounded
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.27 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.27 } 
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.26" # My companion will fight
		event_target:wikid_pirate1 = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_suprize_attacked_pirates } 
				}
				add_trait = wounded
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.27 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.27B } 
		}
	}
}

#Pirate begins the duel vs player or sends to companion to begin

	id = wikid.27
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.27
	picture = GFX_evt_monk_illuminating_book
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
				save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
			}
		}	
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.27" #
		trigger = { FROM = { has_character_flag = wikid_player_vs_pirate } }
		set_character_flag = wikid_pirate_vs_player
		set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
		e_rebels = { holder_scope = { character_event = { id = duel.0 } } }
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.27" #
		trigger = { FROM = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_player_vs_pirate } } }
		set_character_flag = wikid_pirate_vs_companion
		set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
		FROM = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
				set_character_flag = wikid_companion_vs_pirate
				set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
				character_event = { id = wikid.28 }
			}	
		}
	}
}

narrative_event = {
	id = wikid.33
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.33
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.33"

	picture = GFX_evt_merchant_ship_at_sea_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.33" 
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_flag_ship_taken }
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = enormous_flagship }
				remove_character_modifier = enormous_flagship
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = regular_flagship }
				remove_character_modifier = regular_flagship
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = small_flagship }
				remove_character_modifier = small_flagship
			}
			clr_character_flag = flagship_name_SELF
			clr_character_flag = flagship_name_FATHER
			clr_character_flag = flagship_name_SPOUSE
			clr_character_flag = flagship_name_GOD
			clr_character_flag = flagship_name_PROVINCE
			clr_character_flag = flagship_name_DYNASTY
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = wikid_dead_companion
				}
				random_list = {
					100 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.60 days = 30 } 
					}
					#0 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.XXXXXXXX days = 30 } 
					#}
					#0 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.XXXXXXXX days = 30 } 
					#}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_dead_companion }
				}
				random_list = {
					50 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.64 days = 30 } 
					}
					50 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.70 days = 30 } 
					}
					#0 = { narrative_event = { id = wikid.XXXXXXXXXXXX days = 30 } 
					#}
				}
			}
		}	
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.36
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.36 # Tumbler Result
	#title = "EVTTITLEwikid.36" 
	picture = GFX_pillar_lever
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	trigger = { is_alive = yes }

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.36" #Correct
		trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_tumble_correct }	
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = wikid_dead_companion
				}
				narrative_event = { id = wikid.50 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = { has_character_flag = wikid_dead_companion }
				}
				narrative_event = { id = wikid.37 }
			}	
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.36" #incorrect
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_tumble_correct } }	
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler_mad }
			if = { 
				limit = { trait = stressed }	
				if = { 
					limit = { trait = depressed }	
					if = { 
						limit = { trait = possessed }	
						if = { 
							limit = { trait = blinded }	
							if = { 
								limit = { trait = lunatic }	
								random_courtier = {
									limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
									add_trait = has_missing
									death = { death_reason = death_suicide }	
								}
								clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword
								add_trait = has_missing
								death = { death_reason = death_suicide }								
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { NOT = { trait = lunatic } }
								add_trait = lunatic	
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { NOT = { trait = blinded } }
							add_trait = blinded	
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { NOT = { trait = possessed } }
						add_trait = possessed	
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { NOT = { trait = depressed } }
					add_trait = depressed	
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { trait = stressed } }
				add_trait = stressed		
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_tumbler_mad }
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_tumbler_mad		
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = wikid.35 }	
		}	
	}
}

#The Companion - The whore
character_event = {
	id = wikid.38
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.38 # I remember the night we spent together./n/nShe continues;

	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.38"  #It was magical!
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = wikid_whore
			has_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_seduce
		}	
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			add_lover = ROOT
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
					fertility = 0.4
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.4 }
					is_pregnant = no
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { is_female = yes }
					impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
				}	
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no 
						ROOT = { is_pregnant = no }
					}
					ROOT = { impregnate_cuckoo = PREV }
				}
			}	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.43 } }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIPwikidcompanionloves }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.38" #I cant believe you did that, I was an untouched maiden.
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = wikid_whore
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_seduce }
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_read_book }
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
					fertility = 0.4
					ROOT = { fertility = 0.4 }
					is_pregnant = no
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { is_female = yes }
					impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
				}	
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_female = no 
						ROOT = { is_pregnant = no }
					}
					ROOT = { impregnate_cuckoo = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.43 } }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIPwikidcompanionhates }
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCwikid.38" #You read books the whole time and didn't talk to me
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = wikid_whore
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_seduce }
			has_character_flag = wikid_read_book
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.43 } }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIPwikidcompanionhates }
	}
}

#The Companion - Decision
character_event = {
	id = wikid.45
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.45 # 

	picture = GFX_evt_monk_illuminating_book
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.45" #YOU'RE A DICK LETS FIGHT!
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision }
			}	
			set_character_flag = wikid_betrayal_companion
			set_character_flag = flag_duel_to_the_death
			FROM = { 
				set_character_flag = wikid_betrayal_player 
				character_event = { id = wikid.46 }
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision
			}	
			FROM = { 
				set_character_flag = companion_betrayal
			}
			clr_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_betrayal_companion }#You ignored
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 0 }
				NOR = {
					trait = ruthless
					trait = deceitful
					trait = greedy
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -9 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -19 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -29 } }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -39 } }
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -49 } }

				trait = envious
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.45" #YOU'RE A GOOD FELLOW
		if = { #Dragon lair ending
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = dragon_betrayal_decision
			}

			break = yes
		}
		if = { #labyrinth ending
			limit = {

#The Companion - Inform Player Betrayed
character_event = {
	id = wikid.46
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.46 # I will kill you now!
	picture = GFX_evt_lunatic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_ending } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = { ice = { is_alive = yes } }
					dynasty = 59
				}
				FROM = { add_trait = ice }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = { longclaw = { is_alive = yes } }
					dynasty = 102
				}
				FROM = { add_trait = longclaw }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = { blackfyre = { is_alive = yes } }
					or = { 
						dynasty = 57
						dynasty = 496
					}
				}
				FROM = { add_trait = blackfyre }
			}
			if = { # Only if blackfyre already exists
				limit = {
					not = { darksister = { is_alive = yes } }
					blackfyre = { is_alive = yes }
					or = { 
						dynasty = 57
						dynasty = 496
					}
				}
				FROM = { add_trait = darksister }
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					random_province = {
						limit = { has_province_flag = dark_sister_location }
						clr_province_flag = dark_sister_location
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = { brightroar = { is_alive = yes } }
					dynasty = 190

character_event = {
	id = wikid.47
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.47 # 
	#title = "EVTTITLEwikid.47" #A Sad Day
	picture = GFX_evt_illness
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_alive = yes }
				hidden_tooltip = {
					remove_trait = ice
					remove_trait = longclaw
					remove_trait = darksister
					remove_trait = blackfyre
					remove_trait = brightroar
					remove_trait = heartsbane
					remove_trait = nightfall
					remove_trait = ladyforlorn
					remove_trait = redrain
					remove_trait = crabspincer
					remove_trait = strangers_mercy
					remove_trait = vigilance
					remove_trait = orphan_maker
					remove_trait = palemoon
					remove_trait = truth
					remove_trait = lamentation
					remove_trait = poison
					remove_trait = valyrian_steel
					remove_character_modifier = owns_valyrian_steel_sword
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = "EVTOPTAwikid.47"
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_house_words_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = "EVTOPTGETHOUSEWORDS"

				has_house_words_trigger = yes
			}

				random_courtier = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
					death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				}				
			}
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }

##Feast with local noble
narrative_event = {
	id = wikid.84
	title = "EVTTITLEwikid.84" 
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Volantis
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.84A
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				NOR = {
					region = world_jade_sea
					region = world_ghiscar
					region = world_slavers_bay
					duchy = { title = d_volantis }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Astapor
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.84B
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_jade_sea
					region = world_ghiscar
					region = world_slavers_bay
				}
				NOT = { duchy = { title = d_astapor } }
			}
		}
	}
	#generic
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.84C
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					duchy = { title = d_astapor }
					duchy = { title = d_volantis }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.85 days = 5 } } #leave port
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						region = world_jade_sea
						region = world_ghiscar
						region = world_slavers_bay
					}
					NOT = { duchy = { title = d_astapor } }
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					capital_scope = { duchy = { title = d_astapor } } 
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = wikid_feast_host
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					NOT = { duchy = { title = d_volantis } }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { duchy = { title = d_volantis } } }
				save_event_target_as = wikid_feast_host
			}
			break = yes
		}
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { 
				capital_scope = { region = world_slavers_bay } 
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = wikid_feast_host
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.84" #The feast went well
		trigger = {
			event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = -15 }
			}
			NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
		}
		prestige = 25
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enjoyed_feast months = 60 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.84" #It went badly
		trigger = {
			event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = -15 } }
			}
			NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
		}
		prestige = -25
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_dislike }
		}
		event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_dislike months = 60 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCwikid.84" #diplomacy
		trigger = { diplomacy = 10 }
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		prestige = 50
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_wikid_quest_like }
		}
		event_target:wikid_feast_host = {
			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enjoyed_feast months = 60 multiplier = 2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTDwikid.84" #valyrian knowledge
		trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_valyrian }
		prestige = 50
		random_courtier = {

long_character_event = { #Land on cliffs
	id = wikid.94
	picture = GFX_evt_desert
		
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.94
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_cliff_meet_companion }
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_cliff_wreck }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.94B
		trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_cliff_meet_companion } #left companion behind, reunited
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.94C
		trigger = { has_character_flag = wikid_cliff_wreck } #ship wrecked
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.94" #take dangerous route
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { trait = dragon_rider }
			NOT = { trait = crow }
			NOT = { trait = eagle }
		}			
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = wikid_cliff_wreck
				has_character_flag = wikid_flag_ship_taken 
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = enormous_flagship }
				remove_character_modifier = enormous_flagship
			}
			if = {

	id = wikid.102

	desc = EVTDESCwikid.102
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = {
			text = "EVTOPTAwikid.102" 
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_house_words_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = "EVTOPTGETHOUSEWORDS"
			trigger = {
				has_house_words_trigger = yes
			}
		} 
		trigger = { trait = wikid }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = wikid_whore
				has_character_flag = wikid_won_companion_seduce
			}
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
				add_lover = ROOT
				tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { 
						NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
						fertility = 0.4
						ROOT = { fertility = 0.4 }
						is_pregnant = no
					}	
					if = {
						limit = { is_female = yes }
						impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
					}	
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_female = no 
							ROOT = { is_pregnant = no }
						}
						ROOT = { impregnate_cuckoo = PREV }
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		wealth = 500
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.51 days = 60 random = 30 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.51 } #quest ends
		add_character_modifier = { name = owns_valyrian_steel_sword  duration = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { ice = { is_alive = yes } }
				dynasty = 59
			}
			add_trait = ice
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { longclaw = { is_alive = yes } }
				dynasty = 102
			}
			add_trait = longclaw
			break = yes
		}
		if = { # Only if blackfyre already exists
			limit = {
				NOT = { darksister = { is_alive = yes } }
				blackfyre = { is_alive = yes }
				OR = { 
					dynasty = 57
					dynasty = 496

		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.104" 
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
			}
		}	
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			death = { death_reason = death_missing }
		}
		random_friend = {
			limit = { trait = dragon }
			death = { death_reason = death_missing }
		}
		clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword	
		hidden_tooltip = { add_trait = fed_to_dragon }
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = owns_valyrian_steel_sword }
			set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
		}
		death = { 
			death_reason = death_missing
			killer = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

##The Labyrinth
#Path 1
character_event = { 
	id = wikid.110
	picture = GFX_dark_corridor	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.110START
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start 
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.110
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		#If somehow AI is doing this, randomly resolve based on learning
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.66
						NOT = { learning = 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.66
						NOT = { learning = 5 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						learning = 8
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						learning = 11
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						learning = 14
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						learning = 17
					}
					#character_event = { id = wikid. days = 10 }
				}
				20 = {
					random_courtier = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
					random_friend = {
						limit = { trait = dragon }
						random = {
							chance = 50
							death = { death_reason = death_missing }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_modifier = owns_valyrian_steel_sword }
						set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
						custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
					}
					death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword	
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth }
			}
			set_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth
			set_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start
			#6 stages, choice of four pathways, randomise correct pathway at the start for re-playability
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_1_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_2_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_2_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_2_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_2_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_3_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_3_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_3_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_3_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_4_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_4_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_4_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_4_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_5_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_5_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_5_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_5_D }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_A }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_B }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_C }
				1 = { set_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_D }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.110"
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPwikidLABYRINTHA
			hidden_tooltip = {
				clr_character_flag = wikid_labyrinth_start

#Incorrect path
character_event = { 
	id = wikid.111
	picture = GFX_dark_corridor	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111A
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111B
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111C
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111D
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.111E
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		#Five chances before chance of death	
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_1 } }
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_1
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_1
				NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_2 }
			}
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_2
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_2
				NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_3 }
			}
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_3
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_3
				NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_4 }
			}
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_4
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_4
				NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_5 }
			}
			set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_5
			break = yes
		}
		set_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_death
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAwikid.111"
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_death } }	
		random_list = {
			88 = { #safely return to start
				character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						trait = wounded
						is_maimed_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				add_trait = wounded
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					character_event = { id = 38280 } 
					character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
				}
			}
			2 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_maimed_trigger = yes
				}
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBwikid.111"
		trigger = { has_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_death } 
		random_list = {
			70 = { #safely return to start
				character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						trait = wounded
						is_maimed_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				add_trait = wounded
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					character_event = { id = 38280 } 
					character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
				}
			}
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_maimed_trigger = yes
				}
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
				hidden_tooltip = { 
					character_event = { id = wikid.110 days = 1 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.110 }
				}
			}
			5 = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
					death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				}
				random_friend = {
					limit = { trait = dragon }
					random = {
						chance = 50
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_modifier = owns_valyrian_steel_sword }
					set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				clr_global_flag = someone_doing_valyrian_sword	
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_death		
	}
}

		clr_character_flag = labyrinth_path_6_D
		
		clr_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_1
		clr_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_2
		clr_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_3
		clr_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_4
		clr_character_flag = labyrinth_mistake_5
		
		random_courtier = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = wikid_companion }
			save_event_target_as = wikid_companion
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_courtier = {
					has_character_flag = wikid_companion
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.118 }
			break = yes
		}
		narrative_event = { id = wikid.121 }
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

#Character decides to go abroad on adventure
character_event = {
	id = wikid.250
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	min_age = 18
	max_age = 30
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { trait = wikid }
		
		is_ruler = no
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_minor_title = title_triarch }
		OR = {
			is_female = no
			culture_group = hyrkoon_group
		}
		NOT = { trait = content }
		NOT = { trait = slothful }
		liege = { 
			is_close_relative = ROOT
			dynasty = ROOT
			OR = {
				is_patrician = yes
				higher_tier_than = COUNT
			}	
			war = no 
			NOT = { regent = { character = ROOT } }
			is_theocracy = no
		}
		has_epidemic = no
		is_ill = no
		NOT = { has_severe_disability_trigger = yes }
		
		NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
		can_press_claims_trigger = yes
		NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
		NOT = { culture = moon_clansman }
		NOT = { culture_group = free_folk }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = denied_adventure }
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = went_on_foreign_tour }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		#months = 750
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ambition = obj_get_married
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			OR = {
				is_voter = yes
				is_councillor = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_ambition = obj_wants_landed_title
		}

			factor = 10
			trait = hedonist
		}

		modifier = {

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.33
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.33
			trait = cynical
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.33
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.33
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.33
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {

			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.66
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {

#Start the adventure!
character_event = {
	id = wikid.2510
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = foreign_adventure
		add_trait = wikid
		set_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		if = {
			limit = { is_councillor = yes }
			remove_title = job_castellan
			#remove_title = title_hand_of_the_king
			#remove_title = title_hand_of_the_emperor
			remove_title = job_chancellor
			remove_title = job_marshal
			remove_title = job_treasurer
			remove_title = job_spymaster
			remove_title = job_physician
			remove_title = job_spiritual
		}
		character_event = { id = wikid.252 days = 800 random = 400 }
		character_event = { id = wikid.9290 days = 1500 } #end quest failsafe
		#character_event = { id = wikid.252 days = 1 }
		if = { #Chance of proposing foreign marriage
			limit = { 
				can_marry_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = bastard }
				is_female = no
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				modifier = {
					factor = 4
					has_ambition = obj_get_married
				}
				character_event = { id = wikid.274 days = 299 random = 100 }
			}
		}
		#Chance of finding foreign lover
		random = {
			chance = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = lustful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_ambition = obj_find_lover
			}					
			character_event = { id = wikid.280 days = 299 random = 100 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}	
#Adventure outcome selector
character_event = {
	id = wikid.252
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		trait = wikid 
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		if = { #add to seclusion if neccessary
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				prisoner = no
				liege = { has_character_modifier = in_seclusion }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = in_seclusion
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = { #Check adventure can end
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = incapable
					prisoner = yes
					is_ruler = yes
				}
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			break = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			5 = { # Becomes wealthy via trade
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					stewardship = 14
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					stewardship = 18
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.253 } }
			}
			5 = { # Stranded
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.254 } }
			}
			5 = { # Marries foreign peasant

					factor = 0

						is_married = yes
						is_female = yes

						trait = proud
						trait = ruthless
					}						
				}
				modifier = {

					factor = 2
					trait = honorable
				}

				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.261 } }

			5 = { # Captured by Pirates!
				liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.263 } }
			}
			5 = { # Injured
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							trait = rude
							trait = proud

# Becomes wealthy via trade
character_event = {
	id = wikid.253
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.253
	picture = GFX_evt_merchant_ship_at_sea_republic
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { #select random foreign realm for event text
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { trait = wildling }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			random_list = {
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_200 }
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_300 }
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_400 }
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_500 }
				10 = { set_character_flag = trade_750 }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.253	
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_200 }
				prestige = 100
				wealth = 200
				clr_character_flag = trade_200
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_300 }
				prestige = 150
				wealth = 300
				clr_character_flag = trade_300
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_400 }
				prestige = 200
				wealth = 400
				clr_character_flag = trade_400
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_500 }
				prestige = 250
				wealth = 500
				clr_character_flag = trade_500
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = trade_750 }
				prestige = 375
				wealth = 750
				clr_character_flag = trade_750
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_funded_trip } }
				wealth = -100
				ROOT = { wealth = 100 }
			}		
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}			
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

	desc = EVTDESCwikid.254
	picture = GFX_evt_desert
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#select random foreign realm for event text
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.254 #send rescue
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		wealth = -100
		FROM = { 
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure	
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = rescued_my_sorry_ass
				multiplier = 0.5
			}			
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.254 #No
		prestige = -50
		FROM = { 
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_angry
				months = 36
			}
			random_list = {
				35 = {
					
				}	
				20 = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { trait = stressed } }
						add_trait = stressed
					}	
				}
				20 = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ill = no }
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_dlc = "Reapers"
								}
							}
							add_trait = ill
							hidden_tooltip = {
								character_event = {
									id = 38290
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_dlc = "Reapers"
							}
							add_symptom_effect = yes
						}	
					}
				}
				15 = {
					imprison = event_target:foreign_realm
					event_target:foreign_realm = {
						hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.255 } }
					}	
				}
				10 = {
					random_friend = {
						limit = { trait = dragon }
						random = {
							chance = 50
							death = { death_reason = death_missing }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_modifier = owns_valyrian_steel_sword }
						set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
						custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
					}
					death = { death_reason = death_missing }
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = { is_alive = yes }
				remove_trait = wikid
				clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure	
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {					
					create_character = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = none
						female = yes
						religion = PREV
						culture = PREV
						trait = fair
						age = 19
						historical = yes
					}
					new_character = {
						add_spouse = FROM
						add_lover = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = { remove_trait = widowed }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.256
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			prestige = 150
			spouse = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }

			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure	
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}

# Stays abroad
character_event = {
	id = wikid.257
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.257
	picture = GFX_evt_recieve_letter
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#select random foreign realm for event text
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.257
		event_target:foreign_realm = {
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			FROM = { 
				move_character = PREV 
				remove_trait = wikid
				clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
				prestige = 150
				add_character_modifier = { 
					name = went_on_foreign_tour
					duration = -1
				}	
				any_spouse = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						is_ruler = no
						liege = { character = ROOT }
					}
					move_character = PREVPREV
					any_child = {
						limit = {
							is_adult = no
							is_ruler = no
							liege = { character = ROOT }
							is_child_of = PREVPREV	
						}
						move_character = PREVPREVPREV
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_modifier = in_seclusion
						liege = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = in_seclusion } }
					}
					remove_character_modifier = in_seclusion
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.258 } }
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

# Improves Personality
character_event = {
	id = wikid.260
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.260
	picture = GFX_evt_son_asking_father
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { #select random foreign realm for event text
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { trait = wildling }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = humble
					}
					set_character_flag = humble
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = diligent
					}
					set_character_flag = diligent
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = kind
					}
					set_character_flag = kind
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = charitable
					}
					set_character_flag = charitable
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = patient
					}
					set_character_flag = patient
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = brave
					}
					set_character_flag = brave
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = gregarious
					}
					set_character_flag = gregarious
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = just
					}
					set_character_flag = just
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { trait = rude }
					}
					set_character_flag = rude
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { trait = selfish }
					}
					set_character_flag = selfish
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.260
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = humble }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = proud }
					remove_trait = proud
				}
				add_trait = humble
				clr_character_flag = humble
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = diligent }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = slothful }
					remove_trait = slothful
				}
				add_trait = diligent
				clr_character_flag = diligent
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = kind }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = cruel }
					remove_trait = cruel
				}
				add_trait = kind
				clr_character_flag = kind
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = charitable }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = greedy }
					remove_trait = greedy
				}
				add_trait = charitable
				clr_character_flag = charitable
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = patient }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = wroth }
					remove_trait = wroth
				}
				add_trait = patient
				clr_character_flag = patient
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = brave }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = craven }
					remove_trait = craven
				}
				add_trait = brave
				clr_character_flag = brave
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = gregarious }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = shy }
					remove_trait = shy
				}
				add_trait = gregarious
				clr_character_flag = gregarious
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = just }
				if = {
					limit = { trait = arbitrary }
					remove_trait = arbitrary
				}
				add_trait = just
				clr_character_flag = just
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = rude }
				remove_trait = rude
				clr_character_flag = rude
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = selfish }
				remove_trait = selfish
				clr_character_flag = selfish
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			prestige = 150	
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}				
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.265
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.265
	picture = GFX_evt_torture
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { #select random foreign realm for event text
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { trait = wildling }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			}
		}	
		FROM = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = blinded
					}
					set_character_flag = blinded
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = eunuch
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						is_female = yes
					}
					set_character_flag = eunuch
				}
				10 = { 
					set_character_flag = tortured
				}
				10 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						trait = disfigured_AGOT
					}
					set_character_flag = disfigured
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = berserker }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					set_character_flag = craven
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.265
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = blinded }
				add_trait = blinded
				clr_character_flag = blinded
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = eunuch }
				add_trait = eunuch
				clr_character_flag = eunuch
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = tortured }
				add_character_modifier = { 
					name = tortured
					duration = 365
				}
				clr_character_flag = tortured
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = disfigured }
				add_trait = disfigured_AGOT
				clr_character_flag = disfigured
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_character_flag = craven
				}
				add_trait = craven
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}				
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
		}
	}
	
	option = {

# Reaches Asshai
long_character_event = {
	id = wikid.268
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.268
	picture = GFX_asshai
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#select random foreign realm for event text
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.268
		event_target:foreign_realm = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			prestige = 400
			wealth = 350
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}	
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					ai = no
					OR = {
						same_realm = ROOT
						religion_group = ROOT
						dynasty = FROM
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				character_event = { id = wikid.269 }
			}
		}
	}
}

###Mid Quest Events###
# Proposes foreign marriage
character_event = {
	id = wikid.274
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		can_marry_trigger = yes
		NOT = { trait = bastard }
		trait = wikid
		has_character_flag = foreign_adventure
		prisoner = no
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		has_epidemic = no
		liege = {
			is_close_relative = ROOT
			dynasty = ROOT
			higher_tier_than = COUNT
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_playable_ruler = { #find random marriage target
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				ROOT = { 
					liege = { 
						NOT = { lower_tier_than = PREVPREV } 
						is_within_diplo_range = PREVPREV
					} 
				}
				OR = {
					is_patrician = yes
					higher_tier_than = COUNT
				}
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				NOT = { trait = pirate }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				is_theocracy = no
				any_child = {
					is_alive = yes
					is_female = yes
					is_ruler = no
					liege = { character = PREVPREV }
					age = 12
					NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 11 } }
					can_marry_trigger = yes
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { trait = incapable }
					NOT = { trait = bastard }
					has_epidemic = no
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.275 }
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = wikid.275
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.275
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_child = { #find daughter
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_female = yes
				is_ruler = no
				liege = { character = PREVPREV }
				age = 12
				NOT = { age_diff = { who = FROM years = 11 } }
				can_marry_trigger = yes
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = bastard }
				has_epidemic = no
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_marriage_daughter
		}
		FROM = { #find out if needs liege permission
			if = {
				limit = {
					liege = { #Is liege's child or grnadchild
						any_child = {
							OR = {
								character = PREVPREV
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							}
						}
					}
				}	
				set_character_flag = needs_liege_permission
			}	
		}
		#Determine marriage prestige
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
			break = yes
		}
		set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
	}
		
	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAwikid.275 #Yes, Adventurer is free to choose
			trigger = { 
				FROM = { has_character_flag = needs_liege_permission }
			}
		}	
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTBwikid.275 #Yes, Adventurer needs permission
			trigger = { 
				FROM = { NOT = { has_character_flag = needs_liege_permission } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			
			modifier = { #No actual alliance to be gained
				factor = 0.33
				FROM = {
					liege = {
						NOT = { sibling = PREV }
						NOT = { is_child_of = PREV }
					}
					NOT = { has_character_flag = needs_liege_permission }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Would prefer a matrilineal marriage
				factor = 0
				is_patrician = no
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = {
					ROOT = { current_heir = { character = PREVPREV } }
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				religion_group = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { liege = { religion_group = ROOT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = zealous
				FROM = { liege = { NOT = { religion = ROOT } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = zealous
				NOT = { religion = FROM }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				culture_group = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = { liege = { culture_group = ROOT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = proud
				FROM = { liege = { NOT = { culture_group = ROOT } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = proud
				NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				culture = eastern_valyrian
				NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				FROM = { liege = { tier = ROOT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				FROM = { liege = { higher_tier_than = ROOT } }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 40 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 60 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 80 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -19 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -39 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -59 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -79 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -99 } }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FROM = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FROM = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FROM = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FROM = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { FROM = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -24 } } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { FROM = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -49 } } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { FROM = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -74 } } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { FROM = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -99 } } } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_character_flag = needs_liege_permission } } }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					if = {
						limit = { 
							is_betrothed = yes 
						}
						betrothed = {
							if = {
								limit = { is_ruler = yes }
								opinion = {
									who = PREV
									modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = { 
									is_ruler = no 
									liege = { is_close_relative = PREV }
								}
								liege = {
									opinion = {
										who = PREVPREV
										modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
									}
								}	
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = {
				add_spouse = FROM
				# Stop impregnation if too young
				hidden_tooltip = {
					child_fertility_debuff = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { lower_tier_than = DUKE }
				wealth = -25
				FROM = { wealth = 25 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = DUKE }
				wealth = -50
				FROM = { wealth = 50 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = KING }
				wealth = -100
				FROM = { wealth = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
				wealth = -200
				FROM = { wealth = 200 }
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.276 } } } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				prestige = 300
				clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				prestige = 150
				clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
				prestige = 75
				clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35 }
				prestige = 35
				clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = needs_liege_permission } }
			event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
			FROM = { liege = { letter_event = { id = wikid.277 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.277 } } }
		}	
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = needs_liege_permission }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCwikid.275 #No
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = needs_liege_permission }
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
	}
}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { religion_group = ROOT }

				factor = 0.5
				trait = zealous
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { NOT = { religion = ROOT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = zealous
				NOT = { religion = FROM }
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				culture_group = FROM
			}
			modifier = {

				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { culture_group = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = proud
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { NOT = { culture_group = ROOT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = proud
				NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				culture = eastern_valyrian
				NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
			}

				factor = 1.75
				tier = FROM

				opinion = { who = FROM value = 20 }
			}

				opinion = { who = FROM value = 60 }
			}
			modifier = {

				opinion = { who = FROM value = 80 }

				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -19 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -39 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -59 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -79 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -99 } }
			}
		}
		event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { 
			tooltip = { add_spouse = FROMFROM } 
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_betrothed = yes }
				betrothed = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ruler = yes }
						opinion = {
							who = PREV
							modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
						}
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							is_ruler = no 
							liege = { is_close_relative = PREV }
						}
						liege = {
							opinion = {
								who = PREVPREV
								modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
							}
							opinion = {
								who = ROOT
								modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
							}
						}	
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_alliance = { who = FROM years = 10 }
		FROM = { 
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } 
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.278 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { lower_tier_than = DUKE } }
			prestige = 35
			tooltip = {
				wealth = 25
				FROM = { wealth = -25 }
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tier = DUKE } }
			prestige = 75
			tooltip = {
				wealth = 50
				FROM = { wealth = -50 }
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tier = king } }
			prestige = 150
			tooltip = {
				wealth = 100
				FROM = { wealth = -100 }
			}	
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tier = emperor } }
			prestige = 300
			tooltip = {
				wealth = 200
				FROM = { wealth = -200 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.277 #No
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}	
		FROMFROM = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_disappointed
				multiplier = 2
				months = 36
			}
		}
		FROM = { 
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } 
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.279 } }
		}
	}
}
character_event = { #inform foreign ruler accepted
	id = wikid.278
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.278
	picture = GFX_evt_marriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.278
		event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = {
			add_spouse = FROMFROMFROM
			# Stop impregnation if too young
			hidden_tooltip = {
				child_fertility_debuff = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { lower_tier_than = DUKE }
			wealth = -25
			FROM = { wealth = 25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = DUKE }
			wealth = -50
			FROM = { wealth = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = king }
			wealth = -100
			FROM = { wealth = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = emperor }
			wealth = -200
			FROM = { wealth = 200 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
			prestige = 300
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
			prestige = 150
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			prestige = 75
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35 }
			prestige = 35
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
	}
}

# Acquires foreign lover
character_event = {
	id = wikid.280
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		NOT = { trait = widowed }
		NOT = { trait = eunuch }
		NOT = { trait = celibate }
		NOT = { trait = chaste }
		trait = wikid
		has_character_flag = foreign_adventure
		prisoner = no
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		has_epidemic = no
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_playable_ruler = { #find random target
			limit = {
				demesne_size = 1
				NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
				higher_tier_than = DUKE
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { trait = wildling }
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
				NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				any_courtier = {
					is_alive = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							same_sex = ROOT
							trait = homosexual
							ROOT = { trait = homosexual }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
							NOT = { trait = homosexual }
							ROOT = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
						}
						AND = {
							trait = lustful
							ROOT = { 
								trait = lustful
								culture_group = dornish
							}
						}
					}	
					is_ruler = no
					has_lover = no
					is_close_relative = PREV
					liege = { character = PREVPREV }
					age = 16
					NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 11 } }
					prisoner = no
					NOT = { trait = celibate }
					NOT = { trait = incapable }
					NOT = { trait = chaste }				
					opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
					has_epidemic = no
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.281 }
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = wikid.281
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.281
	picture = GFX_evt_viking_throneroom_oldgods
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = { #find lover
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				OR = {
					AND = {
						same_sex = FROM
						trait = homosexual
						FROM = { trait = homosexual }
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { same_sex = FROM }
						NOT = { trait = homosexual }
						FROM = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
					}
				}
				is_ruler = no
				has_lover = no
				is_close_relative = PREV
				liege = { character = PREVPREV }
				age = 16
				NOT = { age_diff = { who = FROM years = 11 } }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = celibate }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = chaste }				
				opinion = { who = FROM value = -20 }
				reverse_opinion = { who = FROM value = -20 }
				has_epidemic = no
			}
			save_event_target_as = foreign_lover
			add_lover = FROM
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.281
		event_target:foreign_lover = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_gracious_host
				months = 120
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.282 } } } }
	}
}

# Attends Feast (also used in player foreign tour)
character_event = { #invitation
	id = wikid.283
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.283
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		trait = wikid
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = foreign_adventure #landless
			has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour #landed			
		}	
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = coming_to_feast }
			had_character_flag = { flag = coming_to_feast days = 180 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.283
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		set_character_flag = coming_to_feast
		hidden_tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_attending_wedding
				months = 12
			}
		}	
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = wikid.284 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.283 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.283 #no
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

	id = wikid.284
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.284
