	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.284
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_ruler = no } }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { liege = { tier = EMPEROR } } }
				prestige = 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { liege = { tier = KING } } }
				prestige = 15
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { liege = { lower_tier_than = KING } } }
				prestige = 5
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { liege = { character_event = { id = wikid.285 } } } }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_ruler = yes } }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tier = EMPEROR } }
				prestige = 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tier = KING } }
				prestige = 30
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { lower_tier_than = KING } }
				prestige = 20
			}
		}	
	}
}

# Becomes party animal
character_event = {
	id = wikid.289
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.289
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = { #select random foreign realm for event text
			limit = { ai = no }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { trait = wildling }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { religion_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				save_event_target_as = foreign_realm
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				set_character_flag = lustful
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = lovers_pox } }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				set_character_flag = minor_disease_herpes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = drunkard } }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				set_character_flag = drunkard
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.289
		FROM = {
			add_trait = hedonist
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = lustful }
				clr_character_flag = lustful
				add_trait = lustful
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = minor_disease_herpes }
				clr_character_flag = minor_disease_herpes
				add_trait = lovers_pox
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drunkard }
				clr_character_flag = drunkard
				add_trait = drunkard
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			piety = -100
			prestige = 150	
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}				
		}
		clear_event_target = foreign_realm
	}
}

#Quest end fail safe
character_event = {
	id = wikid.9290
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.290
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		trait = wikid	
		NOT = { has_character_flag = wikid_quest_started }	
		NOT = { has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour	}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.290
		remove_trait = wikid
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = foreign_adventure }
			clr_character_flag = foreign_adventure
			clr_character_flag = do_not_disturb
			prestige = 150	
			add_character_modifier = { 
				name = went_on_foreign_tour
				duration = -1
			}
		}	
		if = { #add to seclusion if neccessary
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				prisoner = no
				liege = { has_character_modifier = in_seclusion }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = in_seclusion
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Character responds to player quest offer
character_event = {
	id = wikid.292
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
		
	option = {
		name = YES
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				is_primary_heir = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_ambition = obj_get_married
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				plot_target_char = { always = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				plot_target_char = { always = yes }
				plot_target_char = { character = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				OR = {
					is_voter = yes
					is_councillor = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_ambition = obj_wants_landed_title
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = hedonist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = diligent
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = ambitious
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				trait = cynical
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.33
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.4
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.4
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.4
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = wikid.293 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NO
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					is_voter = yes
					is_councillor = yes
					has_ambition = obj_wants_landed_title
					trait = craven
					trait = shy
				}
				OR = {
					trait = hedonist
					trait = diligent
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}
		}	
		set_character_flag = rejected_adventure
		FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = wikid.294 } }
	}
}

			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = wikid.2510 } }
		}		
		prestige = 25
	}
	option = { 
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.293 #Command to find a match
		trigger = {
			higher_tier_than = COUNT
			FROM = {
				is_close_relative = ROOT
				dynasty = ROOT
				can_marry_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = bastard }
				is_female = no
			}
		}
		wealth = -50
		FROM = { 
			tooltip = { add_trait = wikid }
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_funded_trip
				months = 120
			}

				character_event = { id = wikid.2510 } 
			}

# Liege informed relative rejects
character_event = {
	id = wikid.294
	picture = GFX_evt_son_asking_father
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.294
		trigger = {
			FROM = { 
				NOR = {
					is_voter = yes
					is_councillor = yes
					has_ambition = obj_wants_landed_title
					AND = {
						plot_target_char = { always = yes }
						plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
						NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
						NOT = { trait = patient }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.294B
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_ambition = obj_wants_landed_title }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.294C
		trigger = {
			FROM = { 
				NOT = { has_ambition = obj_wants_landed_title }
				OR = {
					is_voter = yes
					is_councillor = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCwikid.294D
		trigger = {
			FROM = { 
				plot_target_char = { always = yes }
				plot_target_char = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
				NOT = { trait = patient }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 	
		name = EVTOPTCwikid.294
	}
}

	desc = EVTDESCwikid.295
	picture = GFX_evt_map
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # More
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.295

# Departed
character_event = {
	id = wikid.298
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.298
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = short_tour }
			character_event = { id = wikid.312 days = 320 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = medium_tour }
			character_event = { id = wikid.312 days = 440 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = long_tour }
			character_event = { id = wikid.312 days = 560 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "tour_stops" value = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { is_councillor = yes }
			remove_title = job_castellan
			remove_title = job_chancellor
			remove_title = job_marshal
			remove_title = job_treasurer
			remove_title = job_spymaster
			remove_title = job_physician
			remove_title = job_spiritual
		}
		if = { #Take flagship?
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = enormous_flagship
					has_character_modifier = regular_flagship
					has_character_modifier = small_flagship
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.334 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = manual_tour }
			event_target:manual_destination_1 = { save_event_target_as = tour_destination }
			clr_character_flag = all_destinations_picked
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_westeros }
			if = {
				limit = { 226 = { has_province_flag = kings_landing_established } }
				226 = { save_event_target_as = tour_destination }
				break = yes
			}
			221 = { save_event_target_as = tour_destination }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_free_cities }
			419 = { save_event_target_as = tour_destination }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_ghiscar }
			625 = { save_event_target_as = tour_destination }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_jade_sea }
			663 = { save_event_target_as = tour_destination }
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_summer_sea }
			496 = { save_event_target_as = tour_destination }
			break = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.298
		add_trait = wikid
		character_event = { id = wikid.303 days = 100 random = 50 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random = { # A terrible storm
				chance = 35
				character_event = { id = wikid.299 days = 40 random = 10 }
			}
			random = { # Attacked by pirates
				chance = 35
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = touring_free_cities
						has_character_flag = touring_summer_sea
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = wikid.301 days = 40 random = 10 }
			}
			character_event = { id = wikid.340 days = 1460 } #clear flags failsafe
		}
	}
}
# A terrible storm
character_event = {
	id = wikid.299
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.299
	picture = GFX_evt_merchant_ship_at_sea_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	option = { # Oh god no
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.299
		random_list = {
			50 = { # Unharmed
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.3
					OR = {
						trait = pirate
						culture = ironborn
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = storm_survive
				character_event = { id = wikid.300 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.299_survive }
			}
			40 = { # Injured
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.8
					has_character_flag = wikid_take_flagship
				}
				set_character_flag = storm_injured
				character_event = { id = wikid.300 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.299_wounded }
			}
			10 = { # Death
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_character_flag = wikid_take_flagship
					has_character_modifier = enormous_flagship
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					has_character_flag = wikid_take_flagship
					has_character_modifier = regular_flagship
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_character_flag = wikid_take_flagship
					has_character_modifier = small_flagship
				}
				random_friend = {
					limit = { trait = dragon }
					random = {
						chance = 50
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_modifier = owns_valyrian_steel_sword }
					set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
					custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPwikidswordlost }
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
			}
		}
	}
}

		trigger = { has_character_flag = storm_injured }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	option = { # Phew
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.300
		trigger = { has_character_flag = storm_survive }
		prestige = 25
		clr_character_flag = storm_survive
	}
	option = { # This better not get infected
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.300
		trigger = { has_character_flag = storm_injured }
		if = { 
			limit = { is_maimed_trigger = yes } 
			health = -1
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { trait = wounded } 
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = wounded }
			add_maimed_trait_effect = yes 
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = wounded }
				NOT = { is_maimed_trigger = yes } 
			}
			add_trait = wounded 
		}
		clr_character_flag = storm_injured
	}
}

# Event selector at destination
character_event = {
	id = wikid.305
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour_alchemist } }
			change_variable = { which = "tour_stops" value = 1 }
		}	
		# Random generic events
		random_list = {
			20 = { # No event
			}
			10 = { # Visit a tavern and get into a brawl
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_character_flag = foreign_tour_brawl_event
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = drunkard
				}

				}

				}

					factor = 0.33
					trait = shy
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.33
					trait = temperate
				}
				set_character_flag = foreign_tour_brawl_event				
				character_event = { id = wikid.314 days = 2 }
			}
			10 = { # Stumble into a brothel

					factor = 0

						trait = celibate
						trait = eunuch
					}
				}

					has_character_flag = foreign_tour_brothel_event
				}

					factor = 2
					trait = lustful
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = hedonist
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.33
					trait = honorable
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					event_target:tour_destination = { holder_scope = { has_character_modifier = owns_a_brothel } }
				}
				set_character_flag = foreign_tour_brothel_event
				character_event = { id = wikid.316 days = 2 }

			10 = { # Visit local nobles and try to make a good impression

					has_character_flag = touring_westeros

					factor = 0.5

			10 = { # Walk through the streets and see peasants/slaves

					factor = 1.5
					has_character_flag = touring_ghiscar
				}
				character_event = { id = wikid.322 days = 2 }
			}
			10 = { # Talk with local traders
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					has_character_flag = touring_free_cities
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_character_flag = foreign_tour_trader_event
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = greedy
				}
				set_character_flag = foreign_tour_trader_event
				character_event = { id = wikid.324 days = 2 }
			}
			10 = { # Some men wish to join you
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					has_character_flag = foreign_tour_men_event
				}
				set_character_flag = foreign_tour_men_event
				character_event = { id = wikid.326 days = 2 }
			}
			10 = { # Make a foreign lover		
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = { 
						trait = celibate
						trait = eunuch
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					has_character_flag = foreign_tour_lover_event
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					has_character_flag = touring_summer_sea
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					has_lover = no
				}
				set_character_flag = foreign_tour_lover_event
				character_event = { id = wikid.328 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_westeros }
			long_character_event = { id = wikid.306 days = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_free_cities }
			long_character_event = { id = wikid.307 days = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_ghiscar }
			long_character_event = { id = wikid.308 days = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_jade_sea }
			long_character_event = { id = wikid.309 days = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = touring_summer_sea }
			long_character_event = { id = wikid.310 days = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = manual_tour }
			long_character_event = { id = wikid.311 days = 5 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

# Move to next desination
character_event = {
	id = wikid.312
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic
	
	desc = { # Next destination
		text = EVTDESCAwikid.312
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = end_tour } }
	}
	desc = { # End tour
		text = EVTDESCBwikid.312
		trigger = { has_character_flag = end_tour }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour_alchemist } }
	
	immediate = {
		clear_event_target = tour_destination
		# Check if tour over
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = short_tour
				check_variable = { which = "tour_stops" value = 3 }
			}
			set_character_flag = end_tour
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = medium_tour
				check_variable = { which = "tour_stops" value = 6 }
			}
			set_character_flag = end_tour
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = long_tour

# Arrive home, also triggered after 320/440/560 days depnding on tour length as you should be done by then anyway
character_event = {
	id = wikid.313
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.313
	picture = GFX_evt_busy_trading_dock_republic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	immediate = { # Clear all character flags
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = manual_tour }
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_1
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_2
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_3
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_4
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_5
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_6
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_7
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_8
			clear_global_event_target = manual_destination_9
			clr_global_flag = someone_doing_manual_tour
		}
		clr_character_flag = touring_westeros
		clr_character_flag = touring_free_cities
		clr_character_flag = touring_ghiscar
		clr_character_flag = touring_jade_sea
		clr_character_flag = touring_summer_sea
		clr_character_flag = manual_tour
		clr_character_flag = short_tour
		clr_character_flag = medium_tour
		clr_character_flag = long_tour
		clr_character_flag = wikid_take_flagship
		clr_character_flag = wikid_no_take_flagship
		clr_character_flag = local_nobles_diplomacy
		clr_character_flag = local_nobles_diplomacy_bad
		
		clr_character_flag = foreign_tour_smith		
		clr_character_flag = foreign_tour_brawl_event
		clr_character_flag = foreign_tour_brothel_event
		clr_character_flag = foreign_tour_nobles_event
		clr_character_flag = foreign_tour_trader_event
		clr_character_flag = foreign_tour_men_event
		clr_character_flag = foreign_tour_lover_event
	}
	
	option = { # What an amazing journey!
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.313
		remove_trait = wikid	
		add_character_modifier = { 
			name = went_on_foreign_tour
			duration = -1
		}
		prestige = 250
		clr_character_flag = do_not_disturb
		clr_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
		if = {
			limit = { trait = stressed }
			remove_trait = stressed
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38313 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = depressed }
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = depressed
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38314 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Visit a tavern and get into a brawl
long_character_event = { 
	id = wikid.314
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.314
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.314 # A fight it is then!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					intrigue = 10
					diplomacy = 10
				}
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.66
					NOT = { combat_rating = 4 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					combat_rating = 6
				}
				set_character_flag = tavern_fight_win
				character_event = { id = wikid.315 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.314_win }
			}
			25 = {
				set_character_flag = tavern_fight_wound
				character_event = { id = wikid.315 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.314_wound }
			}
			5 = {
				random_friend = {
					limit = { trait = dragon }
					random = {
						chance = 50
						death = { death_reason = death_missing }
					}
				}
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

	}

		text = EVTDESCBwikid.315
		trigger = { has_character_flag = tavern_fight_wound }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCCwikid.315
		picture =GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
		trigger = { has_character_flag = tavern_fight_murder }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCDwikid.315
		picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
		trigger = { has_character_flag = tavern_fight_banter }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	option = { # And now I can finish my drink
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.315
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = tavern_fight_win }
			prestige = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = tavern_fight_wound }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					trait = wounded
				}
				hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = wounded }
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { trait = wounded } 
					NOT = { is_maimed_trigger = yes } 
				}
				add_trait = wounded
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38280 } }
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = tavern_fight_win
		clr_character_flag = tavern_fight_wound
		clr_character_flag = tavern_fight_murder
		clr_character_flag = tavern_fight_banter
	}
}
# Stumble into a brothel
character_event = { 
	id = wikid.316
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.316
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	option = { # Well I am here now, may as well have my fun!
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.316
		piety = -25
		if = {
			limit = { 
				trait = chaste 
				NOT = { trait = stressed }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = stressed
				character_event = { id = 38282 }
			}			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
				NOT = { trait = chaste }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = lustful
				character_event = { id = 38272 }
			}		
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { # Possible bastard
			if = {
				limit = {
					fertility = 0.05
					is_female = no
					NOT = { trait = homosexual }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 33
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						NOT = { fertility = 0.25 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						fertility = 0.75
					}
					event_target:tour_destination = { 
						holder_scope = { 
							create_character = {
								random_traits = yes
								dynasty = NONE
								religion = PREV
								culture = PREV
								female = yes
							}
							new_character = { 
								remove_trait = ugly
								random = {
									chance = 25
									add_trait = fair
								}
								remove_trait = chaste
								random = {
									chance = 25
									add_trait = lustful
								}
								save_event_target_as = brothel_mother 
							}
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = wikid.317 days = 274 }
				}
			}	
		}
	}
	option = { # I will not lower myself to that level
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.316
		piety = 25
		if = {
			limit = { 
				trait = lustful 
				NOT = { trait = stressed }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = stressed
				character_event = { id = 38282 }
			}
			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
				NOT = { trait = chaste }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = chaste
				character_event = { id = 38274 }
			}		
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDECCwikid.321
		picture = GFX_evt_valyrian_steel
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = valyrian_smith
			has_character_flag = smith_sword
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDECDwikid.321
		picture = GFX_evt_valyrian_armour
		trigger = { 
			has_character_flag = valyrian_smith
			has_character_flag = smith_armour
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	option = { # A fine sword!
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAwikid.321
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_house_words_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = "EVTOPTGETHOUSEWORDS"
			trigger = {
				has_house_words_trigger = yes
			}
		} 
		trigger = { has_character_flag = smith_sword }
		clr_character_flag = smith_sword
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = valyrian_smith }
			add_trait = valyrian_steel
			add_character_modifier = { name = owns_valyrian_steel_sword  duration = -1 }
			clr_character_flag = valyrian_smith
			break = yes
		}
		add_artifact = sword_tier_2
	}
	option = { # A fine set of armour!
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTBwikid.321
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_house_words_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = "EVTOPTGETHOUSEWORDS"
			trigger = {
				has_house_words_trigger = yes
			}
		} 
		trigger = { has_character_flag = smith_armour }
		clr_character_flag = smith_armour
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = valyrian_smith }
			add_trait = valyrian_armour
			clr_character_flag = valyrian_smith
			break = yes
		}
		add_artifact = fine_armour
	}

character_event = {
	id = wikid.322
	picture = GFX_evt_market
	
	desc = { # Peasants
		text = EVTDECAwikid.322
		picture = GFX_evt_market
		trigger = { 
			event_target:tour_destination = { 
				holder_scope = { 
					NOT = {
						can_buy_courtier_slaves_trigger = yes	
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Slaves
		text = EVTDECBwikid.322
		picture = GFX_evt_slave_market
		trigger = { 
			event_target:tour_destination = { 
				holder_scope = { 
					can_buy_courtier_slaves_trigger = yes	
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	option = { # Give gold to peasant/slave
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.322
		wealth = -15
		piety = 30
		random = { # Host angry for giving cash to commoners
			chance = 25
			character_event = { id = wikid.323 tooltip = TOOLTIPwikid.323 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Buy a slave
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.322
		trigger = { 
			event_target:tour_destination = { 
				holder_scope = { 
					has_full_slavery_trigger = yes	
				}
			}
			can_buy_courtier_slaves_trigger = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = slave_owner } }
			add_trait = slave_owner
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_playable_ruler = {	#Find random ruler to base slave culture on, this is done so not all slaves in the world are clones
				limit = { 
					demesne_size = 1 
					NOT = { culture = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = winter_group }
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
				}
				ROOT = {
					create_character = {
						random_traits = yes
						culture = PREV
						religion = PREV
						dynasty = none
						historical = yes
					}
					new_character = {
						add_trait = slave
						#give_minor_title = title_slave
						opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_my_owner }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_my_slave }
						if = {
							limit = { 
								OR = {
									is_female = no 
									culture_group = hyrkoon_group
								}	
							}
							random_list = {
								40 = { }
								30 = { add_trait = poor_warrior }
								25 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
								5 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
							}				
						}
						if = { #Invalid Kingslander
							limit = {
								226 = { NOT = { has_province_flag = kings_landing_established } }
								culture = crownlander
							}
							culture = riverlander
						}
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		wealth = -35
	}
	option = { # Ignore the commoners
		name = EVTOPTCwikid.322
		piety = -30
		prestige = 15
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = just }
				NOT = { trait = arbitrary } 
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 15
				add_trait = arbitrary
				character_event = { id = 38266 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		}	
	}
	option = { # We have enough people in my party
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.326
		hidden_tooltip = { event_target:wikid.326_new_man = { death = yes } }
	}

# Make a foreign lover
character_event = {
	id = wikid.328
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.328
	picture = GFX_evt_lovers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			holder_scope = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						OR = {
							AND = {
								same_sex = ROOT
								trait = homosexual
								ROOT = { trait = homosexual }
							}
							AND = {
								NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
								NOT = { trait = homosexual }
								ROOT = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
							}
							AND = {
								trait = lustful
								ROOT = { 
									trait = lustful
									culture_group = dornish
								}
							}
						}	
						is_ruler = no
						has_lover = no
						is_married = no
						is_close_relative = PREV
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						age = 16
						NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 11 } }
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = celibate }
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { trait = chaste }				
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
						has_epidemic = no
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
					}	
					save_event_target_as = foreign_lover
					break = yes
				}	
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						OR = {
							AND = {
								same_sex = ROOT
								trait = homosexual
								ROOT = { trait = homosexual }
							}
							AND = {
								NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
								NOT = { trait = homosexual }
								ROOT = { NOT = { trait = homosexual } }
							}
							AND = {
								trait = lustful
								ROOT = { 
									trait = lustful
									culture_group = dornish
								}
							}
						}	
						is_ruler = no
						has_lover = no
						is_married = no
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						age = 16
						NOT = { age_diff = { who = ROOT years = 11 } }
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { trait = celibate }
						NOT = { trait = incapable }
						NOT = { trait = chaste }				
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -10 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -10 }
						has_epidemic = no
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
					}	
					save_event_target_as = foreign_lover
					break = yes
				}	
				capital_scope = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { NOT = { prefers_men_trigger = yes } }
						}
						create_character = {
							random_traits = yes
							dynasty = none
							female = yes
							culture = THIS
							religion = PREV
							historical = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { prefers_men_trigger = yes }
						}
						create_character = {
							random_traits = yes
							dynasty = none
							culture = THIS
							religion = PREV
							historical = yes
						}
					}
					new_character = {
						remove_trait = ugly
						random = {
							chance = 25
							add_trait = fair
						}
						remove_trait = slow
						remove_trait = imbecile
						remove_trait = dull
						remove_trait = chaste
						remove_trait = celibate
						if = {
							limit = { same_sex = ROOT }
							add_trait = homosexual
						}
						move_character = PREVPREV
						save_event_target_as = foreign_lover						
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # I shall ask to meet her in my quarters
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.328
		event_target:foreign_lover = { 
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
			add_lover = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						liege = { is_close_relative = PREV }
						is_married = yes
						is_consort = yes
						is_landed = yes
						has_job_title = yes
						has_minor_title = yes
						is_voter = yes
						trait = kingsguard
						trait = nightswatch
						trait = slave
					}
				}
				move_character = ROOT
			}	
		}
		event_target:tour_destination = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = { id = wikid.329 }
			}
		}
		piety = -50
		if = {
			limit = { is_married = yes }
			piety = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				trait = chaste 
				NOT = { trait = stressed }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = stressed
				character_event = { id = 38282 }
			}			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
				NOT = { trait = chaste }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = lustful
				character_event = { id = 38272 }
			}
			
		}
	}
	option = { # I think not
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.328
		event_target:foreign_lover = { 
			tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
		}	
		piety = 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = lustful 
				NOT = { trait = stressed }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = stressed
				character_event = { id = 38282 }
			}
			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
				NOT = { trait = chaste }
				NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = chaste
				character_event = { id = 38274 }
			}
			
		}
	}

# Offered a marriage from foreign tourist
character_event = {
	id = wikid.331
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.331
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#Determine marriage prestige
		if = {
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Yes, let us bind our families together
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.331
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { #Would prefer a matrilineal marriage
				factor = 0
				is_patrician = no
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = {
					ROOT = { current_heir = { character = PREVPREV } }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				religion_group = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = zealous
				NOT = { religion = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				culture_group = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = proud
				NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				culture = eastern_valyrian
				NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				FROM = { tier = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				FROM = { higher_tier_than = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 40 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 60 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 80 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -19 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -39 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -59 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -79 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -99 } }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						is_betrothed = yes 
					}
					betrothed = {
						if = {
							limit = { is_ruler = yes }
							opinion = {
								who = PREV
								modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { 
								is_ruler = no 
								liege = { is_close_relative = PREV }
							}
							liege = {
								opinion = {
									who = PREVPREV
									modifier = opinion_betrothal_broken
								}
							}	
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = {
			add_spouse = FROM
			# Stop impregnation if too young
			hidden_tooltip = {
				child_fertility_debuff = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { lower_tier_than = DUKE }
			wealth = -25
			FROM = { wealth = 25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = DUKE }
			wealth = -50
			FROM = { wealth = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = KING }
			wealth = -100
			FROM = { wealth = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			wealth = -200
			FROM = { wealth = 200 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
			prestige = 300
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
			prestige = 150
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			prestige = 75
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35 }
			prestige = 35
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = wikid.332 } }
	}
	
	option = { # She will not marry some foreigner
		name = EVTOPTBwikid.331
		FROM = { character_event = { id = wikid.333 } }
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
	}
}
# Marriage accepted
character_event = {
	id = wikid.332
	desc = EVTDESCwikid.332
	picture = GFX_evt_marriage
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	has_character_flag = on_a_foreign_tour
	
	immediate = {
		#Determine marriage prestige
		if = {
			limit = { 
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = emperor } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = king } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { 
					OR = {
						father_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
						mother_even_if_dead = { tier = duke } 
					}	
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			}
			set_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
	}
	
	option = { # A wonderful day!
		name = EVTOPTAwikid.332
		tooltip = {
			event_target:foreign_marriage_daughter = { add_spouse = ROOT }
			if = {
				limit = { lower_tier_than = DUKE }
				FROM = { wealth = -25 }
				wealth = 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = DUKE }
				FROM = { wealth = -50 }
				wealth = 50
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = king }
				FROM = { wealth = -100 }
				wealth = 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tier = emperor }
				FROM = { wealth = -200 }
				wealth = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300 }
			prestige = 300
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_300
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150 }
			prestige = 150
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_150
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75 }
			prestige = 75
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35 }
			prestige = 35
			clr_character_flag = marriage_prestige_35
		}
	}
}
